Request ID - add/generate unique request ID\n17\t// 2. Client IP - extract client IP for rate limiting\n18\t// 3. Logging - log all requests\n19\t// 4. Security Headers - CSP, X-Frame-Options, etc.\n20\t// 5. Rate Limit - per-IP rate limiting\n21\t// 6. CORS - cross-origin support for API\n22\t// 7. Handler - the actual route handler\n23\tfunc Router(cfg *config.Config, log *slog.Logger, rateLimiter *RateLimiter, ch DomainChecker) http.Handler {\n24\t\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n25\t\n26\t\t// Register routes.\n27\t\tregisterRoutes(mux, cfg, log, rateLimiter, ch)\n28\t\n29\t\t// Build middleware chain (applied in reverse order).\n30\t\t// Outer to inner: RequestID -> ClientIP -> Logging -> SecurityHeaders -> RateLimit -> CORS -> Handler\n31\t\thandler := Chain(mux,\n32\t\t\tRequestID,\n33\t\t\tClientIP(cfg.TrustProxy),\n34\t\t\tLogging(log),\n35\t\t\tSecurityHeaders,\n36\t\t\tCORS(cfg),\n37\t\t)\n38\t\n39\t\treturn handler\n40\t}\n41\t\n42\t// registerRoutes adds all routes to the mux.\n43\tfunc registerRoutes(mux *http.ServeMux, cfg *config.Config, log *slog.Logger, rateLimiter *RateLimiter, ch DomainChecker) {\n44\t\t// Create handlers\n45\t\tapiHandlers := NewAPIHandlers(ch, log)\n46\t\twebHandlers := NewWebHandlers(ch, log)\n47\t\n48\t\t// Health check - no rate limiting.\n49\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"GET /health\", healthHandler(log))\n50\t\n51\t\t// Static assets - no rate limiting, cached by browsers.\n52\t\tmux.Handle(\"GET /static/\", http.StripPrefix(\"/static/\", StaticHandler()))\n53\t\n54\t\t// robots.txt at root (served from embedded static).\n55\t\tmux.Handle(\"GET /robots.txt\", robotsTxtHandler())\n56\t\n57\t\t// API routes with rate limiting\n58\t\tmux.Handle(\"GET /api/v1/check\", rateLimiter.APIRateLimit(http.HandlerFunc(apiHandlers.CheckHandler)))\n59\t\tmux.Handle(\"GET /api/v1/check/\", rateLimiter.APIRateLimit(http.HandlerFunc(apiHandlers.CheckHandler)))\n60\t\t// Multi-TLD check endpoint\n61\t\tmux.Handle(\"GET /api/v1/check/multi\", rateLimiter.APIRateLimit(http.HandlerFunc(apiHandlers.MultiTLDHandler)))\n62\t\t// Bulk check endpoint\n63\t\tmux.Handle(\"POST /api/v1/bulk\", rateLimiter.APIRateLimit(http.HandlerFunc(apiHandlers.BulkHandler)))\n64\t\t// Placeholder handler for tlds (Phase 2+)\n65\t\tmux.Handle(\"GET /api/v1/tlds\", rateLimiter.APIRateLimit(http.HandlerFunc(apiHandlers.CheckHandler)))\n66\t\n67\t\t// Metrics endpoint (if enabled).\n68\t\tif cfg.Metrics {\n69\t\t\tmux.HandleFunc(\"GET /metrics\", metricsHandler(log))\n70\t\t}\n71\t\n72\t\t// Web UI routes with web rate limiting.\n73\t\tmux.Handle(\"GET /{$}\", rateLimiter.WebRateLimit(http.HandlerFunc(webHandlers.IndexHandler())))\n74\t\tmux.Handle(\"GET /check\", rateLimiter.WebRateLimit(http.HandlerFunc(webHandlers.CheckHandler())))\n75\t}\n76\t\n77\t// healthHandler returns the server health status.\n78\tfunc healthHandler(log *slog.Logger) http.HandlerFunc {\n79\t\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n80\t\t\thealth := map[string]interface{}{\n81\t\t\t\t\"status\":    \"ok\",\n82\t\t\t\t\"timestamp\": r.Context().Value(RequestIDKey),\n83\t\t\t}\n84\t\t\twriteJSONResponse(w, http.StatusOK, health)\n85\t\t}\n86\t}\n87\t\n88\t// metricsHandler returns Prometheus metrics.\n89\t// Placeholder for Phase 2 - {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_75d77c1bd0dc4258badca2f9","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t// Package server provides the HTTP server with graceful shutdown and middleware.\n2\tpackage server\n3\t\n4\timport (\n5\t\t\"context\"\n6\t\t\"fmt\"\n7\t\t\"log/slog\"\n8\t\t\"net/http\"\n9\t\t\"os\"\n10\t\t\"os/signal\"\n11\t\t\"syscall\"\n12\t\t\"time\"\n13\t\n14\t\t\"github.com/coding/domain-check/internal/config\"\n15\t)\n16\t\n17\t// Server wraps an http.Server with graceful shutdown support.\n18\ttype Server struct {\n19\t\thttp *http.Server\n20\t\tlog  *slog.Logger\n21\t}\n22\t\n23\t// New creates a new HTTP server with the given configuration and handler.\n24\tfunc New(cfg *config.Config, handler http.Handler, log *slog.Logger) *Server {\n25\t\treturn &Server{\n26\t\t\thttp: &http.Server{\n27\t\t\t\tAddr:              cfg.Addr,\n28\t\t\t\tHandler:           handler,\n29\t\t\t\tReadTimeout:       15 * time.Second,\n30\t\t\t\tReadHeaderTimeout: 5 * time.Second,\n31\t\t\t\tWriteTimeout:      30 * time.Second,\n32\t\t\t\tIdleTimeout:       120 * time.Second,\n33\t\t\t\tMaxHeaderBytes:    1 << 20, // 1MB\n34\t\t\t},\n35\t\t\tlog: log,\n36\t\t}\n37\t}\n38\t\n39\t// Run starts the HTTP server and blocks until the server shuts down.\n40\t// It sets up signal handling for graceful shutdown on SIGINT and SIGTERM.\n41\tfunc (s *Server) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n42\t\t// Create a context that is cancelled on SIGINT/SIGTERM.\n43\t\tctx, stop := signal.NotifyContext(ctx, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)\n44\t\tdefer stop()\n45\t\n46\t\t// Start the server in a goroutine.\n47\t\terrCh := make(chan error, 1)\n48\t\tgo func() {\n49\t\t\ts.log.Info(\"server starting\", \"addr\", s.http.Addr)\n50\t\t\tif err := s.http.ListenAndServe(); err != nil && err != http.ErrServerClosed {\n51\t\t\t\terrCh <- err\n52\t\t\t}\n53\t\t}()\n54\t\n55\t\t// Wait for either:\n56\t\t// 1. The server exits with an error\n57\t\t// 2. Request ID - add/generate unique request ID\n17\t// 2. Client IP - extract client IP for rate limiting\n18\t// 3. Logging - log all requests\n19\t// 4. Security Headers - CSP, X-Frame-Options, etc.\n20\t// 5. Rate Limit - per-IP rate limiting\n21\t// 6. CORS - cross-origin support for API\n22\t// 7. Handler - the actual route handler\n23\tfunc Router(cfg *config.Config, log *slog.Logger, rateLimiter *RateLimiter, ch DomainChecker) http.Handler {\n24\t\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n25\t\n26\t\t// Register routes.\n27\t\tregisterRoutes(mux, cfg, log, rateLimiter, ch)\n28\t\n29\t\t// Build middleware chain (applied in reverse order).\n30\t\t// Outer to inner: RequestID -> ClientIP -> Logging -> SecurityHeaders -> RateLimit -> CORS -> Handler\n31\t\thandler := Chain(mux,\n32\t\t\tRequestID,\n33\t\t\tClientIP(cfg.TrustProxy),\n34\t\t\tLogging(log),\n35\t\t\tSecurityHeaders,\n36\t\t\tCORS(cfg),\n37\t\t)\n38\t\n39\t\treturn handler\n40\t}\n41\t\n42\t// registerRoutes adds all routes to the mux.\n43\tfunc registerRoutes(mux *http.ServeMux, cfg *config.Config, log *slog.Logger, rateLimiter *RateLimiter, ch DomainChecker) {\n44\t\t// Create handlers\n45\t\tapiHandlers := NewAPIHandlers(ch, log)\n46\t\twebHandlers := NewWebHandlers(ch, log)\n47\t\n48\t\t// Health check -
